This time I am traveling with children, so I choose the hotel carefully. I hope it has a good view and a good room with some service.
The first thing I want to say is that the charges of this so-called five-star hotel are really dirty! ! ! This is the most dissatisfied part of me. When I took my child there, we asked room service to mop the floor again, and then I wiped the floor myself. The child crawled a little, and when I picked it up, it was still the same as shown in Figure 1. I wiped it myself. The ground, rag and water are all black! ! ! Mosquito corpses are everywhere! ! ! I am really speechless! My husband walked barefoot for a while and his feet were all dirty.
I think cleanliness is a must for this kind of paid hotel, and everything else is secondary. It was so dirty and so careless, which made us very disappointed! ! !
The hotel did say that there is anti-mosquito service. The anti-mosquito service is that the entire hotel is filled with mosquito repellent. The smell is really uncomfortable in the morning, but we don't care. I think if you have children, don't bring it.
Then we ordered Western food for dinner, which cost 298 per person. We still had a little hope. Although the price of 300 for a meal was not very high, it should at least be enough to fill us up. The steak was actually frozen, and Ikea wanted it for 50 a piece. Better, the meat was so white and fluffy. I really didn‚Äôt eat half of it. I admire you for charging such a high price. For the cream of mushroom soup, I repeatedly asked the waiter if there was meat. He told me that there was no meat. After drinking it, I obviously didn‚Äôt know. After eating meat, he asked me to confirm it for me, and it turned out that there was meat!
This so-called Internet celebrity hotel was quite beautiful when I first entered it, but I couldn't get close enough to see it from a distance. The facilities, services, rooms, details, and meals were really not up to par. I was really disappointed this time. Most importantly, The most important thing is hygiene and food. Hygiene is something that the store can do well if they try their best. If the food is really bad, don‚Äôt charge so much. No one‚Äôs money is free. It‚Äôs really speechless and ridiculous. quality.
I hope the store owner will run it with care and put cleanliness first.
